 is yojana ke tahat vaise logon ko aghoshit aay or parisampattiyon ko ghoshit karne kaa mauka diya ja rahaa he, jinhone pehle puure tex kaa bhugtan nahin kiya he

 yojana se judeniyamon kii adhisuchana19 may 2016 ko jari kii gai thi

 yani kul rakam kaa 25 fisadi bhugtan 30 november 2016 tak or agle 25 fisadi kaa bhugtan 31 march 2017 tak iske baad baaki 50 fisadi rakam kaa bhugtan 30 sitambar 2017 tak kiya jayega
 There will be no expansion at the time of the plan, questions have been brought out clarifying the major issues under the rules of the plan
 mantralay ne is baat ko doharaaya gaya he ki 30 sitambar 2016 ko yah yojana band ho rahi he
 There is no case for expansion of this scheme
 aay ghoshit karne waalon se puche jane vaale kuch pramukh sawaal hai-• vaid ghoshnaa kii jaankaree purnat: gopneey rahegi
 It will neither be shared with any law enforcement agency nor will it be investigated by the Income Tax Department
 • is yojana ke tahat ghoshit aay ko 1 june 2016 ke anusaar adhigrahan kii laagat yaa uchit bazaar mulya (donon main jo bhi adhik hoga) ke aadhaar par nirdhaarit kiya jayega

 fat content of healthy ghee

 ye sugar ke marijon ke liye behad phydemand hota he
 Consumption of ghee has been considered safe and healthy for patients with sugar, since ancient times, ghee has been considered a source of healthy fat
 pracheen chikitsakeey upachaaron or kuch adhyayanon main ye suzav diya gaya he ki ghi ko sahi maatra main khaane se hrday rogon kaa kam khatara hota he

 tip tu sugar se peedit logon main ye khatara zyaada hota he
